# Character Changes

- ### ![](images/Aspose.Words.f93ce4e3-25f6-48dc-9813-fc237aafe008.024.png) - LUCINA -

  - General:
    - *Ken can now execute a magic series, being able to cancel moves on shield or on hit. Moves lower in the hierarchy can be canceled into those higher in the hierarchy, in the order of:*

*Light 🠚 Medium 🠚 Heavy 🠚 Command Normal 🠚 Special*

- *Light: jab 1, light dtilt, light utilt*
- *Medium: jab 2, light ftilt, proximity ftilt, heavy dtilt*
- *Heavy: heavy ftilt, heavy utilt, proximity jab, heavy jab, fsmash, up smash, down smash*
- *Command Normal: Oosoto Mawashi Geri, Nata Otoshi Geri*
- *Special: Hadoken, Tatsumaki Senpukyaku, Shoryuken, Focus Attack*
- *In addition, jab 1 can be canceled into light up tilt and light down tilt*
- *Moves are subject to “cancel scaling” - if a move is canceled into via magic series, the move will have altered knockback and less damage*
- *Ken now has a meter system*
  - *Rack up damage to build meter up to a max of 10 levels*
    - *Ken will gain a blue star above his head whenever a meter level is gained*
  - *Meter can be checked by pressing or holding a taunt button at any time; Your current level will be signified by the number of stars above Ken’s head*
    - *Added meter bars are now signified by large, blue stars*
    - *Burned meter bars are now signified by small, transparent stars*
  - *In training mode, meter can be filled instantly by pressing shield during taunt*

- *Terry now has a meter system*
  - *Rack up damage to build meter up to a max of 10 levels*
    - *Added meter levels are signified by a blue star above Terry’s head on meter gain, meter drain will display small transparent stars*

  - *Specials can be canceled into Power Geyser and Buster Wolf on hit for 6 bars of meter*
  - *Power Geyser and Buster Wolf can be canceled into each other respectively for an additional 2 bars of meter*
  - *Specials can be canceled into Triple Geyser by inputting a half-circle forward and Attack/Special for 10 bars of meter*
    - *Triple Geyser can be canceled into from Power Geyser or Buster Wolf for an additional 6 bars of meter*

  - *In training mode, meter can be filled instantly by pressing shield during taunt*
  - *The GO! Meter will appear when Terry has at least four bars of meter*
